## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

### No. 6: Luxury minimalist product photography based on a reference image

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt for generating high-end, minimalist commercial product photography in the style of luxury brand ads, using an uploaded reference image of the core product as the base.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Using my uploaded reference image as the base, generate a minimalist, high-quality commercial still life photograph with the aesthetic of a luxury brand advertisement.

Preserve the general shape, proportions, and main color scheme of the core product in the reference so that it is instantly recognizable as the same product, but upgrade the overall texture and atmosphere of the image, making it look like an ad for a top-tier international fragrance, skincare item, or high-end electronic product.

Use a vertical 4:5 composition. The background should be a large area of clean, neutral negative space, such as soft off-white, cool gray, or light beige, creating a quiet, restrained, and expensive studio environment. Apart from the core product and a minimal number of necessary supports, do not add any extra decorations. No clutter, no elaborate scene setupâ€”only keep very simple geometric supports (such as a plain white cube, a cylinder, or a thin transparent panel). The supports must be simple and low-profile, existing only to hold and accentuate the product.

Strongly emphasize the material details of the product, and let the lighting fully serve those materials:
Show frosted glass with a fine, soft matte texture, ceramics with a matte or slightly glazed feel, and polished metal with clean, sharp specular highlights. Liquids should have clearly visible viscosity and volume. Avoid any cheap plastic feel, complex patterns, or gaudy stickers; the overall material quality must feel cool, restrained, and luxurious.

Use professional studio lighting: mainly soft, diffused light from softboxes, plus precise rim light outlining the productâ€™s shape. The contours should be crisp and layered, and the shadows should be soft and clean, with no noise or dirty shadow patches. You may use a near-macro viewpoint, moving in closer to the product to highlight materials and details, while preserving ample negative space around the frame so the product can "speak for itself" in the emptiness.

Keep the overall color scheme neutral and calm. The productâ€™s own color can be slightly more saturated, making it the single visual focal point in the scene. Do not use exaggerated gradient backgrounds, flashy colored lighting, or e-commerce promo aesthetics. No large-price text, labels, or cartoon graphics.

The final result must be a high-resolution commercial key visual that looks ready for a magazine back cover or a high-end brand announcement poster: minimalist, quiet, high-end, with the core product confidently centered, surrounded by clean negative space and precisely controlled lighting.
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764915823213_skhwpb_G7Qvxi5bIAAqpfX.jpg" width="700" alt="Luxury minimalist product photography based on a reference image - Image 1">
</div>

#### ğŸ“Œ Details

- **Author:** [VoxcatAI](https://x.com/VoxcatAI)
- **Source:** [Twitter Post](https://x.com/VoxcatAI/status/1996273073725780161)
- **Published:** December 3, 2025
- **Languages:** zh

### No. 7: London outdoor restaurant portrait with Nano Banana Pro

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A photorealistic prompt for a young woman at a calm London outdoor restaurant on a crisp March morning, with shallow depth of field and candid phone-photo vibes.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Create a photorealistic image of a young woman sitting at a relaxed outdoor restaurant in {argument name="city in english" default="London"} on a cool Wednesday morning in March {argument name="year in english" default="2025"}. The sky is clear, the spring air is crisp, and the city feels calm as it wakes up. She is the focal point of the shotâ€”wearing a light scarf, gently stirring her tea while gazing off to the side with a thoughtful expression. Everything behind her, from the waiter moving about to the soft morning traffic, should fall into a smooth blur, giving the picture the effortless, candid atmosphere of a moment casually snapped on a phone.
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909307226_bcwb2i_G7QIraQaoAANflM.jpg" width="700" alt="London outdoor restaurant portrait with Nano Banana Pro - Image 1">

### No. 9: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 10: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

]
},

"realistic_details": "natural texture preserved.",
"flash_behavior":"Flash highlights should reveal texture, not hide it."
},

"warmth":"+18",
"contrast":"+22",
"highlights":"-5",

},

"Marble/stone console table with a floral arrangement.",

### No. 8: High-End Conceptual Product Magazine Photography Prompt

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, multi-section prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to generate high-end, glossy magazine editorial photography of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by a specified brand. It includes strict requirements for concept invention, ultra-premium materials, cinematic studio lighting, and precise layout elements like logo and descriptive text placement.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{argument name="Brand Name" default="[Brand Name]"}: 
A high-end, glossy conceptual art magazine editorial photograph showcasing a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by the brand.

**1. Concept and Object (AI Invention):** 
Based on the specified brand's design philosophy, heritage, and material vocabulary, the AI must invent a new type of practical product (not standard clothing, shoes, or bags). Examples may include home goods, tech accessories, tools, or sports equipment, reinterpreted through the brand's perspective. The object should feel sculptural yet functional.

**2. Materials and Details (Ultra High-End):** 
The object is made of high-end, highly tactile materials characteristic of the brand (e.g., oxidized exotic leather, brushed aerospace-grade titanium, sculptural matte ceramic, molded carbon fiber, or technical haute couture textiles). Every detail must be extremely realistic: visible stitching, microscopic material textures, precision engraving, and complex texture contrasts.

**3. Photography and Lighting (Cinematic Studio):** 
Shot with a medium format Phase One camera paired with a 100mm macro lens. Extremely shallow depth of field, with the main object sharply focused and the background blurred to a creamy smoothness. Lighting is exquisite studio softbox illumination: soft, enveloping fill light combined with precise contour light to highlight outlines and material textures.

**4. Environment:** 
Seamless, flawless, pure, ultra-light-toned studio cyclorama background (e.g., desaturated mint green, light pink, or yellowish-white), with no shadows.

**5. Layout and UI Elements (Strict Placement):** 
- **Bottom Right:** The brand's small, low-key, monochromatic gray logo. 
- **Bottom Left:** Small, extremely simple monochromatic gray text describing the invented product. Font style similar to Manrope Regular, with extremely tight tracking (kerning) and balanced line spacing. Example format: "CONCEPT STUDY: [AI inserts invented product name]. MATERIAL: [AI inserts primary material]. SS25."
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed image generation prompt designed for Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro, focusing on creating a photorealistic, high-definition fashion photograph. The prompt specifies the subject's appearance, apparel (a white mini dress), environment (modern interior with a geometric mirror), and aesthetic lighting (warm orange glow), culminating in a concise final generation command.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_analysis": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman with long, straight brunette hair.",
      "expression": "Neutral to confident gaze, looking directly at the camera.",
      "pose": "Standing side-profile, leaning back against a wall, one leg slightly bent (flamingo pose), arms relaxed by her side."
    },
    "apparel": {
      "item": "White mini dress.",
      "style": "Spaghetti straps, fitted bodice, flowy pleated skirt (skater dress style), lightweight fabric."
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Modern interior space.",
      "elements": [
        "Grey wall with vertical alignment.",
        "Large geometric mirror (diamond/diagonal cuts) reflecting the subject's back.",
        "Vertical wall-mounted light fixture."
      ]
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "Ambient and moody.",
      "colors": "Warm orange/reddish glow from the wall light, contrasting with cooler grey tones of the wall.",
      "shadows": "Soft shadows, highlighting the contours of the dress and legs."
    },
    "composition": {
      "framing": "Full body shot.",
      "perspective": "Eye-level.",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on the subject, clear reflection in the mirror."
    }
  },
  "generation_prompt": "A photorealistic full-body shot of a young woman with long {argument name="hair color" default="brown"} hair leaning against a {argument name="wall color" default="grey"} wall, wearing a short {argument name="dress color" default="white"} sleeveless mini dress with a flowy skirt. She is posing in profile with one leg bent. Behind her is a large geometric mirror reflecting her back. To her left is a vertical modern light fixture emitting a warm {argument name="light color" default="orange"} glow. High definition, fashion photography style, aesthetic lighting, 8k resolution, realistic textures."
}

### No. 15: Vintage Evening Flash Portrait Transformation Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extensive JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana, designed for image-to-image transformation. It applies a warm-toned, film-like vintage aesthetic with harsh flash lighting and realistic grain to an input photo, while strictly preserving the subject's facial identity and skin texture (no smoothing or AI alterations).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
"meta":{
"quality":"High-Definition",
"type":"Evening indoor flash portrait",
"ratio":"4:5 vertical",
"device":"iPhone 16 Pro",
"style_reference":"Transform the INPUT PHOTO into this exact aesthetic.",
"look":"Evening flash, warm-toned vintage, real grain, realistic skin texture (NO smoothing)."
},

"identity_lock":{
"preserve_face": true,
"strict": true,
"rules":[
"The face MUST remain IDENTICAL to the input photo.",
"No changes to facial structure, proportions, expression, or identity.",
"No smoothing, no beautify, no retouch, no AI facial alterations."
]
},

"skin_texture_rules":{
"keep_texture": true,
"no_smoothing": true,
"no_blur": true,
"realistic_details": "natural texture preserved.",
"flash_behavior":"Flash highlights should reveal texture, not hide it."
},

"vintage_effect":{
"warmth":"{argument name="warmth" default="+18"}",
"contrast":"{argument name="contrast" default="+22"}",
"highlights":"{argument name="highlights" default="-5"}",
"shadows":"{argument name="shadows" default="+12"}",
"grain":"{argument name="grain" default="Medium (film-like)"}",
"vignette":"{argument name="vignette" default="Soft"}",
"color_grade":"{argument name="color grade" default="Warm beige vintage tint"}",
"sharpness":"{argument name="sharpness" default="Slightly reduced to mimic old camera softness"}"
},

"global_context":{
"scene_description":"{argument name="scene description" default="Indoor hallway with wall decor, mirror reflection, white walls and warm flash lighting."}",
"time_of_day":"{argument name="time of day" default="Evening"}",
"lighting":"{argument name="lighting" default="Direct warm flash illuminating the subject with strong falloff into the background."}",
"environment_details":[
"{argument name="environment detail 1" default="Mirror behind the subject with reflection visible."}",
"{argument name="environment detail 2" default="White paneled walls."}",
"{argument name="environment detail 3" default="Marble/stone console table with a floral arrangement."}",
"{argument name="environment detail 4" default="Soft shadows created by harsh flash."}"
]
},

"composition":{
"camera_angle":"{argument name="camera angle" default="Eye-level, straight-on portrait"}",
"framing":"{argument name="framing" default="Knees-up full portrait"}",
"pose":"{argument name="pose" default="Body leaning slightly forward with one hand on console table and the other arm across the torso."}",
"expression":"{argument name="expression" default="Confident, pouty, soft glamorous gaze."}",
"flash_effect":"{argument name="flash effect" default="Glossy highlights on skin and dress."}"
},

"subject":{
"makeup":{
"style":"{argument name="makeup style" default="Soft glam."}",
"lips":"{argument name="lips" default="Pink-brown gloss with warm undertone."}",
"eyes":"{argument name="eyes" default="Eyeliner + lashes."}",
"blush":"{argument name="blush" default="Warm peach."}"
},
"skin":"{argument name="skin" default="Natural undertone, realistic texture, NOT smoothed."}",
"outfit":{
"dress":"{argument name="dress" default="White mini halter dress with deep neckline and satin-like shine."}",
"fabric_behavior":"{argument name="fabric behavior" default="Flash creates bright reflections and visible folds."}"
}
},

"background_objects":[
{
"id":"mirror",
"description":"{argument name="mirror description" default="Large wall mirror reflecting the subject's pose."}",
"lighting":"{argument name="mirror lighting" default="Flash reflection visible but subdued."}"
},
{
"id":"flowers",
"description":"{argument name="flowers description" default="Vibrant bouquet on the table (yellow, purple, green)."}"
},
{
"id":"wall",
"description":"{argument name="wall description" default="White paneled wall with framed signage."}"
}
],

"rules":{
"identity_constant": true,
"no_face_change": true,
"no_ai_artifacts": true,
"realism":"{argument name="realism" default="Ultra realistic evening flash aesthetic with vintage tones."}"
}
}
Use the uploaded photo as the input image. Generate the image.
```

### No. 26: Culinary Periodic Table Display Board Generator

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex instructional prompt designed to generate a visual representation of a dish's flavor profile in the style of a scientific periodic table. It requires analyzing a dish's ingredients and flavor compounds, then rendering a detailed display board with color-coded compartments, molecular structures, and a handwritten recipe, combining chemistry aesthetics with product design.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
<instruction> 
Input A is a famous dish (photo or dish name). Analyze the dish's complete ingredient breakdown, primary flavor compounds, chemical interactions, and scientific basis for why ingredients work together.
Optional Input B is a style reference (laboratory equipment / tech product packaging). If missing, choose scientific periodic table meets Apple product design aesthetic.
Goal: Grid-format display board (20"x16") in periodic table structure, with each ingredient in its own compartment labeled with both culinary and scientific information, color-coded by flavor profile.
Rules:

Brushed aluminum, white acrylic, or frosted glass backing
20-30 small clear compartments in periodic table grid layout
Each compartment contains: ingredient specimen, common name, scientific name, primary flavor molecule
Color-coded borders: umami (red), sweet (pink), sour (yellow), bitter (green), fat (orange), aromatic (purple)
Center "legend" section: 3D molecular structure diagram of signature compound
Lower corner: actual handwritten recipe on aged vellum or parchment under glass
AR markers for scanning to see animated 3D molecule models
Clean sans-serif typography (like Helvetica or Futura)
Minimal design with generous white space
Include atomic-style "numbers" for each ingredient showing ratio/importance

Output: ONE image, 4:5 clean product photography style with soft shadows on pure white background
</instruction>
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed image generation prompt for Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro, requesting an extreme close-up macro photograph of a Beagle drinking water. The prompt focuses on capturing the precise action (tongue curled into a spoon shape), hyper-realistic textures (wet nose, fur), and the visual elements of the water (ripples, turquoise tint), using a shallow depth of field for artistic focus.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{

    "subject": {
      "type": "Dog",
      "breed": "Beagle",

        "fur_color": "Golden-tan and white",
        "eyes": "Large, expressive, amber-brown, intense gaze",

        "ears": "Floppy, golden-brown (partially out of frame)"
      }
    },
    "action": {
      "primary": "Drinking water",
      "details": [
        "Tongue extended downward",
        "Tongue curled backward into a spoon shape (ladling)",
        "Creating small splashes and ripples",
        "Water droplets falling from the mouth"
      ]
    },
    "composition": {
      "framing": "Extreme close-up / Macro",
      "angle": "Low angle, water-level view",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on the eyes, snout, and tongue; shallow depth of field blurring the ears and background",
      "alignment": "Center-aligned face"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Water surface (pool or large bowl)",
      "water_appearance": "Clear, turquoise/aquamarine tint, reflective, rippled texture"
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "Natural daylight",

      "highlights": "Reflections on the wet nose, eyes, and water surface"
    },

      "color_palette": [

#### ğŸ“– Description

    "replace_identity_only": true,
    "preserve_body_proportions": true,

  },

      "yaw": 2
    },
    "grip": "fingers_wrapped_thumb_along_edge"

### No. 37: E-Girl Mirror Selfie with Deep Depth of Field

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly technical JSON prompt for generating an 'E-Girl Mirror Selfie' with a minimalist goth style. It specifies engine configuration, including LoRA slots and sampling settings, but its core instruction is to enforce a deep depth of field (f/11) so that the subject, bed texture, and background wall are all sharp, contrasting the typical shallow depth of field in portraits.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "meta": {
    "project": "Egirl_FrogPose_PinkHK_Flux_V4.2",
    "target_engine": "Flux.1 [dev] / Nano Banana Pro",
    "version": "4.2.0 (Everything in Focus - f/11)",
    "created_at": "2025-12-18T20:55:00Z"
  },
  "engine_configuration": {
    "model": {
      "base": "flux1-dev.safetensors",
      "quantization": "fp8 / nf4",
      "vae": "ae.safetensors"
    },
    "lora_slots": [
      {
        "name": "Realism_LoRA_v2 (Optional)",
        "strength": 0.5,
        "note": "Enhances porcelain skin tone and fabric textures."
      }
    ],
    "sampling": {
      "sampler_name": "euler",
      "scheduler": "simple",
      "steps": 28,
      "guidance_scale": 2.5,
      "shift": 1.0
    },
    "dimensions": {
      "width": 1024,
      "height": 1536,
      "aspect_ratio": "2:3",
      "megapixel_class": "1.5MP"
    }
  },
  "prompt_construction": {
    "narrative_layer": {
      "style": "E-Girl Mirror Selfie / Minimalist Goth",
      "instruction": "Capture a sharp, full-body mirror selfie of a young woman sitting in a frog pose on a bed, focusing on the midriff and the pink phone case.",
      "subject_flow": "A pale 19-21 year old woman with black wolf-cut hair sitting on a grey bed with knees up, holding a pink Hello Kitty phone."
    },
    "texture_layer": {
      "skin_physics": "pale porcelain skin, smooth texture, rosy blush, glossy lips, e-girl eyeliner",
      "fabric_physics": "ribbed knit texture of black tube top, metal grommets on belt, cotton texture of white socks, quilted grey duvet",
      "environment_physics": "SHARP DETAILS ON BACKGROUND: glass mirror reflection, white wall texture, window glass, grey fabric folds"
    },
    "camera_physics": {
      "lens_imperfections": "smartphone camera aesthetic, high fidelity",
      "focus": "DEEP DEPTH OF FIELD (f/11) - NO BLUR. The woman, the bed texture, and the background wall are all sharp.",
      "settings": "Smartphone Simulation, 24mm Lens, 1/60s, ISO 300 (Diffused Window Light)"
    },
    "color_grading": {
      "white_balance": "Cool Natural (Diffused Window Light)",
      "shadows": "Soft shadows defining the midriff",
      "highlights": "Soft highlights on skin and glossy phone case"
    }
  },
  "final_prompt_string": "A candid raw mirror selfie photograph shot on Smartphone f/11. Deep depth of field, everything in focus. A very slim 19-21 year old woman with pale porcelain skin and black hair with bangs (wolf cut) sitting on a dark grey bed in a 'frog pose' (knees bent, high and wide apart). She leans back slightly. She wears a black ribbed strapless tube top exposing her toned midriff, a low-rise black mini skirt with a heavy silver grommet belt, and white ankle socks with red Hello Kitty embroidery. She holds a phone with a light pink 3D Hello Kitty case. Dramatic e-girl eyeliner and glossy lips. Background is sharp and detailed: messy grey duvet and a plain white wall are clearly visible with no bokeh. "
```

### No. 41: Photorealistic Portrait with Shallow Depth of Field

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly specific prompt for generating a photorealistic portrait of a young Asian woman in a black pinstriped shirt dress and sheer thigh-high stockings. It details the pose, environment (sheer curtains), lighting (warm, soft indoor), and precise camera settings (focal length, aperture, shutter speed, ISO) to achieve a shallow depth of field and a polished, slightly candid aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A photorealistic portrait of a young Asian woman with voluminous, long, wavy black hair and fair skin. She is wearing thin-rimmed, round glasses and has a playful expression, winking one eye with a subtle smile. Outfit: She is dressed in a black, long-sleeved button-down shirt dress with thin white vertical pinstripes. She is wearing sheer black thigh-high stockings. Pose: She is seated in a curved, cream-colored leather armchair. Her body is angled slightly forward. Her right hand is raised, with long manicured fingers delicately touching her cheek and jawline in a playful, posing gesture. Environment: The background features soft, floor-length beige or off-white sheer curtains, suggesting an indoor hotel room or bedroom setting at night. Lighting & Style: Warm, soft indoor lighting that creates gentle highlights on her hair and the silky texture of the shirt. High-resolution photography, sharp focus on the face, slightly candid but polished aesthetic. Camera Angle: Slightly high angle (tilted down about 10â€“15 degrees), seated eye-level. Focal Length: 35mm or 50mm. (This creates a natural perspective without too much distortion, typical of high-end smartphone portraits or standard portrait lenses). Aperture: f/2.0 to f/2.8. (This provides a shallow depth of field, keeping her face and hand in sharp focus while softly blurring the texture of the curtains in the background). Shutter Speed: 1/60s or 1/100s. (Standard for indoor handheld shots to avoid motion blur). ISO: 400 to 800. (Slightly higher sensitivity to account for the warm, dim indoor lighting without introducing too much grain). Lighting Setup: Soft key light from the front-top (likely a ceiling fixture or ring light), creating the specular highlights on the nose and forehead.
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed JSON prompt for generating a photograph of a marble sculpture in the style of 19th-century Neo-Classical or Romantic artists like Canova or Rodin. It specifies the subject (a mythological embrace with wet drapery), the material (Carrara marble with aged patina), the museum gallery setting, and the soft, diffused lighting designed to highlight the stone's texture and form.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

{
  "art_medium": {
    "type": "Sculpture, photograph of",

    "artist_reference": "style of Antonio Canova or Auguste Rodin (softer, more emotive)",
    "material": "white Carrara marble with a slightly aged patina",
    "presentation": "photographed in a museum gallery setting"

        "type": "A beautiful female figure, a nymph or goddess",

        "clothing": "draped in very thin, flowing fabric that clings revealingly to her body contours (wet drapery technique), partially falling off her shoulder"
      },

        "type": "A male figure (like Cupid or a youth) or just hands",

        "clothing": "nude or with minimal drapery"
      }
    },
    "composition": "The figures are intertwined, creating a sense of intimate connection and movement frozen in stone."
  },

      "the sculpture rests on a large, ornate carved stone plinth",
      "the background is a soft-focus, textured wall with architectural moldings",
      "other blurred classical busts and pedestals are visible in the distance"
    ],
    "atmosphere": "quiet, reverent, sensual, artistic"
  },
  "lighting_and_color": {
    "type": "Soft, diffused gallery lighting",
    "source": "overhead skylight or large window from the side",
    "effect": "highlighting the smooth, cold texture of the marble and casting soft shadows in the folds of the drapery, creating a three-dimensional effect",
    "palette": "monochromatic shades of white, cream, and warm greys"
  },
  "technical_specs": {
    "composition": "photograph of a sculpture, eye-level view",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:2 horizontal",

  }
}

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro, originally built on a ChatGPT prompt, designed for ultra-photorealistic image generation. It focuses on generating a mirror selfie of a young woman in a black saree and modern blouse, strictly preserving her facial and body identity from a reference image, and aiming for an editorial yet natural look with realistic fabric physics and skin texture.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "type": "{argument name="type" default="image_generation"}",
  "model_style": "{argument name="model style" default="ultra_photorealistic"}",
  "aspect_ratio": "{argument name="aspect ratio" default="9:16"}",
  "resolution": "{argument name="resolution" default="8K"}",
  "quality": "{argument name="quality" default="high_detail_realism"}",
  "identity_reference": {
    "use_reference_image": true,
    "face_preservation": "{argument name="face preservation" default="exact"}",
    "body_preservation": "{argument name="body preservation" default="exact"}",
    "no_facial_changes": true,
    "no_body_modification": true
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "{argument name="gender" default="female"}",
    "age": "{argument name="age" default="young adult"}",
    "expression": "{argument name="expression" default="soft confident gaze, natural lips slightly parted"}",
    "pose": "{argument name="pose" default="slightly angled mirror selfie pose, relaxed shoulders, natural posture"}",
    "hair": {
      "color": "{argument name="hair color" default="dark brown"}",
      "style": "{argument name="hair style" default="loose, natural volume, middle part"}",
      "texture": "{argument name="hair texture" default="smooth and realistic"}"
    },
    "skin": {
      "tone": "{argument name="skin tone" default="warm natural complexion"}",
      "detail": "{argument name="skin detail" default="visible skin texture, realistic highlights, no plastic look"}"
    }
  },
  "outfit": {
    "style": "{argument name="outfit style" default="black saree with modern blouse"}",
    "blouse": "{argument name="blouse" default="black sleeveless blouse with subtle shimmer embroidery"}",
    "saree": "{argument name="saree" default="black draped saree with soft fabric folds and realistic fabric physics"}",
    "accessories": [
      "{argument name="accessory 1" default="delicate waist chain"}",
      "{argument name="accessory 2" default="minimal jewelry"}"
    ]
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "{argument name="location" default="indoor modern bedroom or dressing area"}",
    "background": "{argument name="background" default="clean white wardrobe cabinets"}",
    "lighting": {
      "type": "{argument name="lighting type" default="soft indoor lighting"}",
      "source": "{argument name="lighting source" default="overhead ceiling light"}",
      "effect": "{argument name="lighting effect" default="natural shadows, balanced highlights"}"
    }
  },
  "camera": {
    "device": "{argument name="device" default="smartphone"}",
    "lens": "{argument name="lens" default="natural portrait lens"}",
    "angle": "{argument name="angle" default="slightly above eye level"}",
    "focus": "{argument name="focus" default="sharp focus on subject, mild background softness"}",
    "depth_of_field": "{argument name="depth of field" default="realistic"}"
  },
  "rendering_rules": {
    "no_cartoon": true,
    "no_ai_artifacts": true,
    "no_over_smoothing": true,
    "no_extra_limbs": true,
    "no_distorted_hands": true,
    "no_text_or_watermark": true
  },
  "final_look": "{argument name="final look" default="looks like a real candid photo, ultra-realistic, editorial yet natural"}"
}

### No. 51: Cozy Work-From-Home Selfie Image Generation Prompt

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured and detailed prompt for generating a realistic photo of a young woman working from home. It specifies the subject's appearance (clear glasses, chunky knit sweater), the environment (wooden desk, natural daylight from a window with a city view), and the objects present (laptop, notebook, mug), aiming for a cozy, academic, work-from-home aesthetic.

    },

    },

    },
    "objects": [
      "open laptop (MacBook style)",
      "document or text editor visible on screen",
      "open notebook",
      "pen",
      "ceramic mug (beige/white)"
    ],
    "style": "realistic, selfie angle, casual, cozy, academic, work-from-home aesthetic"
  },
  "prompt": "A realistic photo of a young woman with long dark wavy hair wearing clear glasses and a chunky cream knit sweater, sitting at a wooden desk near a window. She is smiling gently at the camera. In front of her is an open laptop displaying a document, a notebook with a pen, and a ceramic mug. ### No. 53: Ultra-Modern Transparent Black Hyperrealism

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured JSON prompt for generating hyperrealistic 3D objects in an ultra-modern, futuristic style using transparent black glass or polymer. It emphasizes high-gloss finish, sharp specular highlights from rim and directional lighting, and a pure dark void background to showcase the floating, minimalistic design of objects like a lighter, microphone capsule, and camera lens element.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{

    "target_style": {

        "sleek",
        "futuristic",
        "minimalistic",
        "floating design",
        "high-gloss transparency"
      ],
      "material_appearance": {
        "base_material": "transparent black glass or polymer",
        "texture_quality": "smooth and curved",
        "finish": "high-gloss with partial internal reflections"
      }
    },

    "objects": [
      "transparent black lighter with visible inner structure",
      "glass microphone capsule floating",
      "black glass camera lens element",
      "minimal glass joystick / control stick"
    ]
  },

  "lighting_style": {
    "source_type": "rim light and directional top light",
    "intensity": "high",
    "shadows": "soft and diffuse glow underneath",
    "highlight_behavior": "sharp specular highlights and reflections across transparent surfaces"
  },

  "color_palette": {
    "dominant_colors": ["#000000", "#0d0d0d", "#1a1a1a"],
    "accent_colors": ["#ffffff", "#333333"],
    "contrast_level": "very high",
    "overall_tone": "dark, glossy, and luminous"
  },

  "rendering_style": {
    "dimensionality": "3D hyperrealistic",
    "resolution_quality": "ultra high",
    "depth_effects": "floating volumetric space with layered reflections"
  },
  "output_settings": {
    "aspect_ratio": "1:1",

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex JSON prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro designed for image-to-image generation, focusing on creating an ultra-realistic POV shot looking down at a MacBook screen. The screen displays a Photo Booth live preview of the subject (whose identity is strictly preserved from the input photo) in a dim bedroom, with Spotify running in the background. The prompt emphasizes realism details like RGB pixel grids, dust, and natural noise, simulating a photo taken of a screen rather than a screenshot.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_settings": {
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "resolution": {
      "width": 1152,
      "height": 1536
    }
  },

  "prompt": {
    "identity_lock": {
      "reference": "{argument name="reference" default="input_photo"}",
      "preserve": [
        "{argument name="preserve 1" default="face"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 2" default="facial proportions"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 3" default="eye shape"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 4" default="nose"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 5" default="lips"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 6" default="skin tone"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 7" default="skin texture"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 8" default="hairline"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 9" default="overall identity"}"
      ],
      "rules": [
        "{argument name="rule 1" default="no face swap"}",
        "{argument name="rule 2" default="no beautify"}",
        "{argument name="rule 3" default="no smoothing"}",
        "{argument name="rule 4" default="no reshaping"}",
        "{argument name="rule 5" default="no AI look"}"
      ]
    },

    "scene": {
      "camera_angle": "{argument name="camera angle" default="high-angle downward shot, POV"}",
      "composition": "{argument name="composition" default="MacBook screen fills most of the frame, thin strip of physical keyboard visible at the bottom"}",
      "screen_surface": [
        "{argument name="screen surface 1" default="visible RGB pixel grid"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 2" default="subtle moire effect"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 3" default="micro dust on glass"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 4" default="faint fingerprints"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 5" default="soft ambient reflections"}"
      ]
    },

    "digital_interface": {
      "os": "{argument name="os" default="macOS dark mode"}",
      "background_app": {
        "name": "{argument name="background app name" default="Spotify"}",
        "view": "{argument name="background app view" default="Liked Songs"}",
        "visible_tracks": [
          "{argument name="track 1" default="Blank Space â€“ Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 2" default="Shake It Off â€“ Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 3" default="Cruel Summer â€“ Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 4" default="Love Story â€“ Taylor Swift"}"
        ]
      },
      "foreground_app": {
        "name": "{argument name="foreground app name" default="Photo Booth"}",
        "state": "{argument name="foreground app state" default="live preview window"}",
        "position": "{argument name="foreground app position" default="floating, center-right"}"
      }
    },

    "photo_booth_content": {
      "environment": {
        "room": "{argument name="room" default="dim bedroom"}",
        "background": "{argument name="background" default="off-white wall, rumpled bedding"}",
        "lighting": "{argument name="lighting" default="low-light, nocturnal, cool screen glow mixed with warm skin tones"}"
      },
      "subject": {
        "pose": "{argument name="subject pose" default="lying down, relaxed, candid"}",
        "expression": "{argument name="subject expression" default="natural, slightly relaxed"}",
        "outfit": "{argument name="subject outfit" default="light-colored tank top"}",
        "prop": {
          "item": "{argument name="prop item" default="iPhone 15 Pro"}",
          "hand": "{argument name="prop hand" default="right hand"}"
        }
      }
    },

    "realism_rules": [
      "{argument name="realism rule 1" default="this is a photo of a screen, not a screenshot"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 2" default="raw smartphone photo look"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 3" default="natural noise"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 4" default="imperfect glass"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 5" default="no studio lighting"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 6" default="no HD polish"}"
    ]

### No. 59: Three Identity-Locked Photorealistic Portraits

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A collection of three distinct prompts, all focused on generating highly photorealistic portraits while strictly preserving the facial identity of an uploaded reference image. They cover different styles: an extreme close-up beauty shot, a cinematic travel portrait in a snowy alpine train, and a retro vintage 90s look with a red dress and flowers.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Prompt 1:
"A hyper-realistic, extreme close-up beauty portrait of a stunning woman. She is raising her arm to cover the left side of her face, wearing a vibrant red ribbed-knit sweater. Only one mesmerizing hazel-green eye is visible, featuring dramatic black winged eyeliner, gold glitter eyeshadow, and long lashes. Her lips are full and painted with a matte red lipstick that matches the sweater perfectly. Flawless airbrushed skin, soft studio lighting, high fashion editorial style, sharp focus on the eye no facial change same as it is on the reference picture."

Prompt 2:
"Create a highly photorealistic, cinematic travel portrait of a young woman whose facial identity exactly matches the uploaded reference image, with 100% preservation of facial structure, proportions, skin texture, eye shape, lips, nose, brows, moles, and natural expression. She has a soft, relaxed smile with calm eyes and is gently looking toward the camera. Her pose shows her leaning out of a train window, with both arms resting comfortably on the window frame and her upper body slightly leaned forward in a relaxed, cozy posture.
She has dark brown straight hair worn loose and slightly tucked under a white knitted winter beanie with a soft knit texture. Her makeup is natural winter-style, featuring an even fair skin tone, light blush, soft eyeliner, natural lashes, and subtle pink lips. She is wearing a cream or off-white cozy winter sweater made of soft, warm knit fabric suitable for cold weather.
The scene is set inside a red panoramic train traveling through snowy alpine mountains. The background includes snow-covered pine trees, mountain slopes blanketed in snow, curving red train cars visible behind her, and thick snow piled along the tracks, clearly conveying a winter landscape. Lighting is natural cold daylight with soft diffusion, cool winter tones, gentle highlights on the face, and natural shadows.
The overall style is a cinematic travel portrait with a DSLR photography look, moderate depth of field that keeps the subject sharp while preserving scenic background detail, and a peaceful, cozy, adventurous winter travel mood. Use high-resolution rendering with realistic skin texture, high detail, and cool winter color grading with soft contrast, maintaining strict identity lock to the reference image throughout."

Prompt 3:
"Create A hyper-realistic person (Retro vintage, grainy but bright aesthetic. A girl(face exactly same as the reference image) wearing a perfect red wine colored red frock, holding a A bunch of 10-12 flowers of roses in her hands. The style feels like a 90s movie, romantic, wind blowing girl. She is standing against a solid wall with deep shadows and dramatic contrast, mysterious and artistic atmosphere."
```

### No. 62: Travel Itinerary Illustration Generation Prompt

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 'hand-drawn travel itinerary' illustration based on a character reference image. It includes sections for customizable input (character features, title, destination, schedule, and packing list) and strict specifications for the image generation style, layout (vertical A4, grid background, timeline composition), content reflection (5-6 small cut illustrations per schedule item, character consistency, expression reflection), and decorative elements.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate an illustration image in the style of a travel itinerary according to the following requirements.

## 1. Input Settings
** (Please rewrite this section. If left blank, it will be treated as "Leave it to AI")**
- **Character Features**: {argument name="Character Features" default="A girl with brown short hair, wearing a black cloak"}
- **Name (for Title)**: {argument name="Name for Title" default="Complete Guide to the Donut Museum!"}
- **Tourist Destination**: {argument name="Tourist Destination" default="Donut Museum"}
- **Schedule**: [
Format: "Time : Place/Action : Short Comment (Situation or Feeling at the time)"
]
- **Packing List**:

## 2. Image Generation Specifications
You are an illustrator for a travel magazine. Based on the settings above, draw one "hand-drawn travel itinerary" in the following style.

**ã€Style and Compositionã€‘**
- **Aspect Ratio**: Vertical (Vertical format close to A4 paper ratio)
- **Background**: Graph paper (grid notebook) texture.
- **Art Style**: Warm, hand-drawn style illustration like the reference image (watercolor, marker, colored pencil touch).
- **Layout**:
- Place the title prominently at the top.
- Timeline composition connected by arrows flowing from the top left to the bottom right.
- Memo illustration of the "Packing List" in the bottom right or an empty space.

**ã€Content and Comment Reflectionã€‘**
- Draw each item in the specified "Schedule" as **5-6 small cut illustrations**.
- Maintain **character consistency**.
- **Comment Reflection**:
- Reflect the content of the "Short Comment" in the schedule in the character's **expression and pose** (e.g., if "delicious," the cheeks should be relaxed; if "excited," the eyes should sparkle).
- Place a **handwritten-style text space (like a speech bubble, sign, or writing in the margin)** next to or below each panel for the comment.
- *The text in the image must be accurate Japanese. Use a font that looks like handwritten notes.*

**ã€Decorationã€‘**
- Overall cheerful and pop atmosphere.
- Decorate with masking tape, stamps, handwritten arrows, and musical note marks.
```

### No. 63: Anamorphic Graphite Sketch Illusion Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly complex image generation prompt for Nano-Banana Pro, designed to create a photorealistic image of a graphite sketch that appears to be reaching out of the paper (anamorphic illusion). The prompt requires a reference image for the subject's identity and details the artistic style, demanding monochromatic greyscale for the subject and realistic colors for the surrounding drawing tools and rustic wooden desk.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "subject_core": {
    "demographics": "[STRICTLY FOLLOW REFERENCE IMAGE]: Age, gender, and ethnicity must match the uploaded source photo exactly. Rendered as a hyper-realistic graphite sketch.",
    "body_type": "Matches reference image physique, appearing to lean forward out of the 2D plane",
    "facial_features": "High-fidelity graphite translation of the reference face; shading emphasizes specific bone structure and unique traits from the source photo; eyes detailed with paper-white catchlights",
    "hair": "Matches reference image hairstyle and texture exactly, rendered with varying pencil pressure (hatching and cross-hatching)"
  },
  "subject_styling": {
    "makeup_grooming": "Matches reference image grooming standards; skin texture converted to realistic pencil grain and stippling",
    "expression": "Matches reference image expression (e.g., focused, smiling, or neutral), intense gaze directed relative to the viewer",
    "pose_action": "Anamorphic illusion: The subject's hand (drawn in graphite) creates a 3D effect, appearing to reach out of the flat paper surface, holding a realistic wooden pencil"
  },
  "wardrobe": {
    "top": "Matches clothing from reference image, textures converted to graphite cross-hatching to imply fabric weight",
    "bottom": "N/A (cropped or fading into the white of the paper)",
    "footwear": "N/A",
    "accessories": "Any distinct accessories from the reference photo rendered in sketch format"
  },
  "environment_context": {
    "location": "Macro view of a textured, heavy-tooth white sketchbook page resting on a dark rustic wooden surface",
    "background_elements": "Real-world objects resting on the paper to sell the scale: a worn white block eraser, a metal pencil sharpener, scattered cedar wood pencil shavings, smudge of graphite dust",
    "time_context": "Studio lighting environment, timeless artistic setting"
  },
  "cinematography_and_tech": {
    "lighting": "Dual lighting setup: 1. Simulated shading within the sketch based on the reference. 2. External 'real world' harsh lamp light casting long shadows from the pencil and eraser onto the paper",
    "camera_gear": "Macro photography, 100mm lens, sharp focus on the paper texture",
    "framing": "Top-down flat lay or slight isometric angle to enhance the 'pop-up' 3D illusion of the sketch",
    "visual_fidelity": "Photorealistic rendering of paper grain/fiber, tactile graphite sheen, rough charcoal texture, high contrast between dark leads and white paper",
    "color_grading": "Monochromatic greyscale for the subject (graphite/charcoal tones), natural realistic colors for the desk and drawing tools"
  },
  "aspect_ratio": "4:5"
}
```

</div>

### No. 65: Playful Shaving Cream Mirror Selfie Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed image generation prompt for Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro 3.0, aiming to create a high-contrast, playful mirror selfie of a couple covered in white shaving cream. The prompt specifies the composition, lighting (moody, low-key), and the authentic social media aesthetic, including a negative prompt list to ensure quality.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "subject": {
    "description": "A playful, high-contrast mirror selfie of a young couple completely covered in thick, white shaving cream.",
    "individuals": [
      {
        "gender": "male",
        "position": "background, looking toward the camera with a deadpan, slightly skeptical expression",
        "features": "sculpted shaving cream forming 'horns' or ears on his head"
      },
      {
        "gender": "female",
        "position": "foreground, holding a smartphone and pouting her lips in a 'duck face'",
        "features": "visible eyeliner, manicured nails with a french tip style, looking up toward the other person"
      }
    ],
    "texture": "heavy, whipped, peaks of foam, matte white lather"
  },
  "composition": {
    "type": "close-up mirror selfie",
    "framing": "medium shot, waist-up",
    "focal_point": "the texture of the shaving cream and the interaction between the two faces",
    "elements": "a black smartphone with a white MagSafe ring and a small rectangular sticker is held in the foreground"
  },
  "lighting_and_color": {
    "lighting": "moody, low-key lighting with a strong directional light source creating deep shadows",
    "color_palette": "dominant cool blues in the background, stark white foam, natural skin tones peeking through",
    "contrast": "high contrast between the bright white foam and the dark, navy blue background"
  },
  "technical_details": {
    "style": "authentic social media aesthetic, candid photography",
    "camera_feel": "mobile phone camera quality, slight grain, shallow depth of field",
    "atmosphere": "playful, chaotic, artistic, youthful"
  },
  "negative_prompt": "clean skin, professional studio lighting, bright background, blurry, distorted hands, messy hair"
}

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A photorealistic image generation prompt for the Gemini app's Nano Banana Pro model. The objective is to create an emotionally warm, tight close-up portrait of a woman (whose identity must be preserved from a reference image) and a silver tabby kitten peeking out from under a sheet of paper with the word 'happy' handwritten on it, emphasizing soft lighting and shallow depth of field.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "Objective": "Generate a realistic, emotionally warm close-up portrait featuring a woman and a silver tabby kitten interacting under a sheet of paper.",

    "Scene_Description": "A close-up portrait of a woman (matching the appearance of the uploaded reference image) and a silver tabby kitten.         "Expression": "Soft, calm, and affectionate",
        "Pose": "Face close to the kitten, head slightly tilted toward it"
      },
      "Kitten": {
        "Breed": "{argument name="kitten breed" default="Silver tabby"}",
        "Eyes": "Large, round, dark brown eyes expressing curiosity",
        "Nose": "Small and pink",
        "Expression": "Curious and gentle"
      }
    },
    "Props_and_Elements": {
      "Paper": {
        "Type": "Sheet of paper or newspaper",
        "Position": "Covering the top of both heads",
        "Edge_Detail": "Slightly curved top edge",
        "Text": "The word '{argument name="text on paper" default="happy"}' written on the left side in an informal, handwritten style"
      }
    },
    "Composition": {
      "Framing": "Tight close-up portrait",
      "Focus": "Sharp focus on faces, especially eyes",
      "Depth_of_Field": "Shallow depth of field"
    },
    "Background": {
      "Color": "Light gray or white",
      "Style": "Blurred and minimalist"
    },
    "Lighting_and_Style": {
      "Lighting": "Soft, natural light with gentle highlights",
      "Mood": "Warm, tender, and serene",
      "Art_Style": "Photorealistic"
    },
    "Quality_Settings": {
      "Resolution": "High resolution",
      "Detail_Level": "Ultra-detailed facial and fur textures"
    }
  },

### No. 79: Victorian Gothic Royal Portrait Magazine Cover Prompt

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed, multi-section prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate a 9:16 vertical, realistic magazine cover photo in a 'Victorian Gothic Royal' style. It requires 100% identity preservation from an uploaded face reference, specific heavy-duty Victorian court attire, London landmarks as the background, cinematic lighting, complex color matrix selection, and specific poses suitable for a magazine cover.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate a 9:16 vertical, realistic photo of a "Victorian Gothic Royal" portrait: Use the uploaded FACE_REF as the character identity reference, 100% restoring the facial features and bone structure; the person is wearing heavy-duty court attire in the style of the "Victorian Era (19th Century) Court Gown" (corset, large crinoline, lace/velvet, royal jewelry), photographed next to the Tower Bridge or the Palace of Westminster (Big Ben) in London. The image should have photography, styling, and cover design quality comparable to 'Harperâ€™s Bazaar', maintaining the magazine's consistent design style (Chinese and English design).

ã€INPUTS | Inputã€‘
FACE_REF: Uploaded facial feature reference image (identity lock)

ã€ABSOLUTE PRIORITY | Identity Lock (Highest Priority)ã€‘
100% restoration of FACE_REF's facial features and bone structure: Eye distance, nose bridge and wings, lip shape, jawline, and cheekbone structure must be completely consistent, with no deviation.
Realistic skin texture: Visible subtle textures and pores; avoid excessive smoothing or 'influencer' filters.
Adult female image (adult).

ã€SHOT TYPE | Two View Options (Model randomly selects one, must be realistic and consistent)ã€‘
A) Half-body cover: From the chest to above the waist, with jewelry, lace neckline, and eyes being the clearest (Primary recommendation)
B) Full-body cover: Complete presentation from head to toe, showing the full silhouette of the huge crinoline combined with the London landmark, strong perspective (Alternative)
(Regardless of A/B: Must maintain a "cover composition," with white space reserved for typography, but without torn paper/hand-drawn effects.)

ã€LOCATION | Scene (London, UK)ã€‘
London Landmark: By the River Thames, with the magnificent Gothic architecture of the Palace of Westminster (Big Ben) or the Tower of London Bridge in the background.
Weather option (random): 1) London Fog (classic foggy texture, soft and mysterious light) 2) Just after rain (wet ground reflection, lead-gray sky)
Clean background: No tourists, no modern signs, no mobile phone status bar UI, no watermarks or subtitles.

ã€LIGHTING & CAMERA | Photographic Quality (Magazine Grade)ã€‘
Lens feel: 85mm portrait quality (half-body) or 50mm/70mm (full-body), shallow depth of field, eyes are the sharpest.
Lighting: Overcast diffused light + dramatic fill light (emphasizing facial structure); diamonds/gems must have realistic fire; velvet texture must be deep.
Color: High-end cinematic feel, low-saturation blue-gray environment combined with the dark tones of the clothing (red/blue/black) to form a Gothic aesthetic; overall clean, transparent, and luxurious.

ã€WARDROBE | Victorian Court Gown (Heavy-duty, Sculpting, Intricate Details)ã€‘
Target aesthetic: "Wasp waist, large skirt, layered lace, heavy velvet, crown, queenly aura."

Silhouette and Layers (X-shaped tailoring)
Upper body: Highly structured corset, square or high neckline, puff sleeves or leg-of-mutton sleeves
Lower body: Huge crinoline or bustle, with noticeable stacking design at the back waist, skirt trailing on the ground
Decoration: Abundant ruffles, bows, dangling tassels
Fabric and Craftsmanship (Heavy craftsmanship must be "visible")
Main fabric: Heavy velvet, taffeta, Chantilly Lace
Main techniques: Beading, gold thread embroidery, ribbon weaving
Pattern themes: Damask, roses, thistle (symbol of Scotland), paisley pattern
Details: Lace gloves, neck ornament (Choker), medal/brooch
Headwear (Royal Jewelry Headpiece)
Core structure: Victorian small crown (Tiara) or feather headpiece
Decoration: Diamonds, sapphires, pearls
Earrings/Necklace: Extremely exaggerated diamond necklace, drop earrings

ã€COLOR MATRIX | Color Matrix Pairing (Must be executed, and must be "Royal Dark Colors")ã€‘
(Deep luxury of the late Victorian era)
Randomly select 1 set from the following three "Main Color Schemes" for the [Base Color/Large Area Main Fabric Color].

Scheme G (Royal Blue Base):
Base Color: Deep sapphire blue/midnight blue (velvet texture)
Embroidery/Decoration: Silver lace, diamonds, sapphires
Scheme A (Victorian Red Base):
Base Color: Wine red/Burgundy red (deep passion)
Embroidery/Decoration: Black lace, gold embroidery, rubies
Scheme R (Mourning Black Base):
Base Color: Ink black (Black Jet, extremely Gothic)
Embroidery/Decoration: Black beads, black lace, small amounts of gold or silver highlights

ã€Color Execution Rulesã€‘
Colors must be deep and rich, reflecting the majesty of the "Empire on which the sun never sets" and Gothic mystery.

ã€POSE | Cover Pose (Majestic, Stiff, Queenly Aura)ã€‘
Half-body: Chin slightly raised, cold gaze, one hand gently touching the necklace
Full-body: Standing tall (like a portrait painting), hands clasped on the crinoline, overwhelming presence
Expression: Serious, arrogant, imperious; absolutely no smiling (Victorian style).

ã€OUTPUT | Outputã€‘
1 vertical 9:16 realistic magazine cover photo
Random: Half-body or Full-body (A/B selection)
Random: Fog or Rain (Weather selection)
Random: Sapphire Blue / Wine Red / Ink Black (Color matrix selection)
Styling: Victorian court gown direction + Crown/Choker + Corset and large crinoline + Velvet and lace
```

### No. 83: Four-Panel Collage with Strict Identity and Pose Matching

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed JSON prompt designed to generate a 2x2 collage of images, requiring 100% identical facial structure, pose, angle, and expression matching from an uploaded reference image. The prompt specifies different views (front, back, mirror selfie, side portrait) and details the subject's Asian ethnicity, outfit (vintage blue floral dress), accessories, and romantic vintage lifestyle aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "reference": {
      "face_identity": "uploaded reference image",
      "identity_lock": true,
      "pose_lock": true,
      "camera_angle_lock": true,
      "expression_lock": true,
      "face_preservation": "100% identical facial structure, proportions, eyes, lips, nose, brows, skin texture"
    },

    "composition": {
      "layout": "2x2 collage",
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "pose_matching": "exactly match reference image poses, angles, framing, and body orientation",
      "no_variation_allowed": true
    },

    "panel_1": {
      "view": "front-facing portrait",
      "pose": "head slightly tilted, eyes toward camera, soft lips",
      "framing": "chest-up selfie angle",
      "expression": "calm, elegant",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_2": {
      "view": "back view",
      "pose": "standing facing mirror, arms raised slightly",
      "focus": "back of head and bow hairstyle",
      "framing": "upper-body rear shot",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_3": {
      "view": "mirror selfie",
      "pose": "phone covering part of face, body angled sideways",
      "framing": "waist-up",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "panel_4": {
      "view": "side portrait",
      "pose": "head turned over shoulder looking into camera, holding bouquet close to chest",
      "expression": "soft romantic gaze",
      "framing": "upper torso",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "subject": {
      "gender": "female",
      "ethnicity": "Asian",
      "skin_tone": "fair with soft blush"
    },

    "hair": {
      "style": "long straight hair, half-up",
      "accessory": "large cream ribbon bow",
      "placement": "exact position as reference image"
    },

    "outfit": {
      "dress": {
        "color": "white",
        "pattern": "blue floral print",
        "style": "vintage puff-sleeve dress",
        "neckline": "square neckline"
      },
      "jewelry": [
        "pearl necklace",
        "delicate gold pendant"
      ]
    },

    "environment": {
      "location": "vintage-style indoor room",
      "background": [
        "ornate mirror",
        "cream walls",
        "soft floral decor",
        "classic furniture"
      ],
      "match_reference_background": true
    },

    "lighting": {
      "type": "soft indoor daylight",
      "quality": "even, gentle, warm",
      "shadow": "minimal",
      "match_reference": true
    },

    "photography_style": {
      "style": "romantic vintage lifestyle",
      "lens": "DSLR portrait lens",
      "depth_of_field": "shallow",
      "color_grading": "soft pastel"
    },

    "render_quality": {
      "realism": "photorealistic",
      "resolution": "high",
      "texture_detail": "natural skin and fabric detail",
      "no_cartoon": true
    }
  }
}
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

### No. 92: Polished Indoor Portrait with Shallow Depth of Field

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for generating a photorealistic, polished portrait of a young Asian woman with glasses, seated in a leather armchair. The prompt specifies her outfit (pinstripe shirt dress, thigh-high stockings), pose (winking, hand near cheek), and precise camera settings (35mm/50mm, f/2.0-f/2.8) to achieve a shallow depth of field and warm indoor lighting.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Subject: A photorealistic portrait of a young Asian woman with voluminous, long, wavy black hair and fair skin. She is wearing thin-rimmed, round glasses and has a playful expression, winking one eye with a subtle smile.
Outfit: She is dressed in a black, long-sleeved button-down shirt dress with thin white vertical pinstripes. She is wearing sheer black thigh-high stockings.
Pose: She is seated in a curved, cream-colored leather armchair. Her body is angled slightly forward. Her right hand is raised, with long manicured fingers delicately touching her cheek and jawline in a playful, posing gesture.
Environment: The background features soft, floor-length beige or off-white sheer curtains, suggesting an indoor hotel room or bedroom setting at night.
Lighting & Style: Warm, soft indoor lighting that creates gentle highlights on her hair and the silky texture of the shirt. High-resolution photography, sharp focus on the face, slightly candid but polished aesthetic.
Camera Angle: Slightly high angle (tilted down about 10â€“15 degrees), seated eye-level.
Focal Length: 35mm or 50mm. (This creates a natural perspective without too much distortion, typical of high-end smartphone portraits or standard portrait lenses).
Aperture: f/2.0 to f/2.8. (This provides a shallow depth of field, keeping her face and hand in sharp focus while softly blurring the texture of the curtains in the background).
Shutter Speed: 1/60s or 1/100s. (Standard for indoor handheld shots to avoid motion blur).
ISO: 400 to 800. (Slightly higher sensitivity to account for the warm, dim indoor lighting without introducing too much grain).
Lighting Setup: Soft key light from the front-top (likely a ceiling fixture or ring light), creating the specular highlights on the nose and forehead.
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed image generation prompt for Nano Banana Pro, requesting a cinematic close-up of elegant hands writing the Arabic phrase 'Ù„ØºØªÙŠ Ù‡ÙˆÙŠØªÙŠ' (My language is my identity) on textured parchment paper. #### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A cinematic close-up of elegant hands writing the Arabic phrase "{argument name="arabic phrase" default="Ù„ØºØªÙŠ Ù‡ÙˆÙŠØªÙŠ"}" with a traditional ink pen on textured parchment paper. ### No. 103: Diverse Fashion Editorial Grid

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex prompt designed to generate a 6x6 grid of 36 unique individuals wearing the same reference clothing item. The prompt explicitly maximizes human diversity across age, body type, ethnicity, hair, and facial features, requiring varied poses and camera angles to create an inclusive, high-contrast fashion editorial.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
6x6 grid layout. Editorial fashion photography. Use the reference clothing item on all 36 models. Every single cell must feature a completely unique individualâ€”no two people should look remotely similar.
Maximize human diversity across:
Age: Teenagers, 20s, 30s, 40s, 50s, 60s, 70s, 80s+, elderly with wrinkles and grey hair
Body types: Extremely thin, slim, athletic, muscular, stocky, chubby, fat, plus-size, obese, petite, tall, short, broad-shouldered, narrow-framed, pear-shaped, apple-shaped, hourglass, rectangular, long-limbed, short-limbed.
Ethnicity & skin tones: East Asian, Southeast Asian, South Asian, Middle Eastern, North African, Sub-Saharan African, West African, East African, Indigenous Australian, Pacific Islander, Native American, Indigenous South American, Scandinavian, Mediterranean, Eastern European, Western European, Caribbean, mixed race, albino. Full spectrum of skin tones from the palest to the deepest.
Hair: Bald, shaved, buzz cut, afro, locs, braids, straight, wavy, curly, coily, long, short, grey, white, natural colors, receding hairline, thinning hair, thick full hair, hijab, head wraps, turbans.
Features: Freckles, vitiligo, acne, scars, birthmarks, moles, gap teeth, crooked teeth, big nose, small nose, wide nose, narrow nose, round face, angular face, soft jawline, strong jawline, monolid eyes, deep-set eyes, hooded eyes, big lips, thin lips, visible disabilities, prosthetics, wheelchair users, amputees.
Each cell: different pose, different camera angle. Poses should feel editorial and unexpectedâ€”leaning, crouching, mid-stride, arched, sprawled, seated, jumping, twisting, lounging. Camera angles varyâ€”low angle, overhead, Dutch tilt, wide shot, tight crop, ground-level, profile, three-quarter view.
Moody, high contrast, cinematic lighting. Varied environmentsâ€”studio, architectural, urban, natural. Sharp detail, clothing as focal point. Final result should feel like the most inclusive, human-rich fashion editorial ever createdâ€”a true celebration of every single type of human body that exists.
```

    }

### No. 111: Image to Fragmented Stone Sculpture Style Transfer

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured JSON prompt for Nano Banana PRO to perform an image-to-image style transfer, transforming the main subject of an uploaded photo into a hyper-realistic, fragmented stone assemblage. It specifies material details (slate and sandstone shards), lighting (soft studio key light), and strict identity preservation.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "task": "image_to_image_style_transfer",
  "input_image": "{{USER_IMAGE}}",
  "prompt": "Create a hyper-real 3D studio composition that recreates the main subject from the provided image as a fragmented stone assemblage. The subject must be built from separate, clearly detached rock pieces with small visible gaps between shards (no pieces merging). Material look: fragmented slate + sandstone shards with chiseled edges, crisp fractures, visible stone grain, micro-scratches, and realistic roughness. Color palette: predominantly dark slate with subtle warm-ochre sandstone accents. Lighting: soft studio key light from top-left, gentle fill, subtle contact shadows under each shard, realistic ambient occlusion in crevices, clean reflections kept minimal. Background: minimal off-white seamless backdrop, no texture. Framing: centered, clean, straight-on, subject fully readable. Add a few tiny debris chips floating or resting near the base for depth. Preserve the subjectâ€™s identity, proportions, and recognizable silhouette from the input image while transforming all surfaces into stone fragments. Hyper-real, high detail, sharp focus, 8k render quality.",
  "negative_prompt": "text, typography, logo, watermark, signature, extra props, busy background, fog, heavy bloom, cartoon, illustration, lowpoly, plastic, metal, glossy paint, melted shapes, merged fragments, unreadable subject, blur, noise, low resolution, oversharpening halos, distorted face/body, extra limbs, deformed geometry",
  "output": {
    "aspect_ratio": "use_input_aspect_ratio",
    "background": "off_white",
    "camera": {
      "angle": "straight_on",
      "framing": "centered",
      "distance": "medium"
    }
  },
  "params": {
    "style_strength": 0.75,
    "identity_preservation": 0.9,
    "detail_level": "very_high",
    "lighting_preset": "soft_studio_top_left",
    "shadow_intensity": "subtle",
    "gap_visibility": "clear",
    "debris_chips": "few_tiny",
    "no_text": true
  }
}

### No. 117: Ultra-Realistic 8K Candid Street Portrait

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON prompt designed to generate an ultra-realistic 8K candid street portrait of a thoughtful young woman in a crowded urban environment, emphasizing shallow depth of field, warm cinematic tones, and documentary street photography aesthetics.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "Objective": "Create an ultra-realistic 8K candid street portrait capturing quiet emotion and authenticity within a crowded urban environment.",

  "Subject": {
    "Gender": "Female",
    "Appearance": {
      "Hair": "Short blonde hair with soft, natural texture",
      "Makeup": "Minimal, natural look",
      "Skin": {
        "Texture": "Realistic skin texture with subtle freckles",
        "Highlights": "Soft natural highlights with gentle tonal transitions"
      },
      "Expression": "Calm, thoughtful, introspective",
      "Gaze": "Looking slightly to the side, not directly at the camera"
    },
    "Wardrobe": {
      "Top": "Simple grey knitted sweater with visible fabric weave",
      "Bottom": "Casual jeans",
      "Accessories": "Thin shoulder-bag strap visible across the shoulder"
    }
  },

  "Scene_Description": {
    "Setting": "Busy city street",
    "Crowd": {
      "Density": "Surrounded by a dense flow of pedestrians",
      "Background_Treatment": "Softly blurred figures creating depth and motion"
    },
    "Environment": "Urban street atmosphere with natural movement"
  },

  "Lighting_and_Color": {
    "Lighting": {
      "Type": "Natural daylight",
      "Quality": "Soft and even, without harsh shadows"
    },
    "Color_Grading": {
      "Style": "Warm cinematic tones",
      "Characteristics": [
        "Natural skin tones",
        "Muted urban background colors",
        "Subtle film-inspired contrast"
      ]
    }
  },

  "Camera_and_Composition": {
    "Shot_Type": "Candid street portrait",
    "Depth_of_Field": "Shallow depth of field isolating the subject",
    "Focus": "Sharp focus on the subject with background crowd softly blurred",
    "Angle": "Eye-level, unobtrusive framing"
  },

  "Visual_Style": {
    "Resolution": "Ultra-realistic 8K",
    "Aesthetic": "Documentary street photography",
    "Detail_Characteristics": [
      "Sharp facial detail",
      "Natural fabric texture",
      "Soft motion blur in background",
      "Subtle film grain for realism"
    ]
  },

  "Mood_and_Storytelling": {
    "Themes": [
      "Stillness within chaos",
      "Quiet reflection",
      "Human presence in urban life"
    ],
    "Atmosphere": "Emotional, authentic, understated realism"
  },

  "Output_Requirements": {
    "Format": "Image",
    "Orientation": "Portrait or cinematic street frame",
    "Quality": "Professional documentary-grade realism"
  }
}
```

### No. 118: Clean Girl Aesthetic Selfie in Upscale Apartment (JSON Format)

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed JSON prompt for generating a photorealistic selfie of a young woman in an upscale, modern apartment, capturing the 'clean girl' aesthetic. It specifies the subject's appearance (dark wavy hair, dewy skin, minimalist gold jewelry), the environment (open floor plan, wood cabinets, cream sofa, potted plants), and technical details (iPhone 17 Pro Max, natural daylight, medium close-up framing).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "prompt_data": {
    "subject_description": {
      "demographics": "Young woman, approximately early 20s, Caucasian",
      "hair": "Long, dark brown, loose wavy texture, center part, voluminous",
      "eyes": "Hazel/light brown, direct eye contact, captivating gaze",
      "skin": "Fair complexion, dewy finish, flawless texture",
      "face_features": "High cheekbones, defined jawline, full lips with soft pink gloss, natural eyebrows",
      "expression": "Neutral, soft, alluring, confident"
    },
    "outfit_and_accessories": {
      "clothing": "Sleeveless deep V-neck top or dress",
      "fabric_texture": "Suede or soft velvet material",
      "color": "Taupe / Light Brown / Beige",
      "jewelry": "Minimalist thin gold choker necklace"
    },
    "environment_and_background": {
      "setting": "Modern upscale apartment interior, open floor plan",
      "kitchen_area": {
        "cabinets": "Vertical grain wood finish",
        "appliances": "Stainless steel microwave and oven combo",
        "lighting": "Modern metal dome pendant light",
        "countertops": "White/Light stone"
      },
      "living_area": {
        "furniture": "Cream/White textured sofa or sectional",
        "decor": "Large indoor potted green plants (Ficus/Fiddle Leaf)",
        "flooring": "Light wood flooring",
        "walls": "White, clean architectural lines"
      }
    },
    "technical_specs": {
      "camera_model": "iPhone 17 Pro Max",
      "camera_angle": "Selfie perspective from front-facing camera, arm extended, eye-level",
      "framing": "Medium close-up, chest up",
      "lighting": "Soft natural daylight, diffused indoor lighting, even illumination on face, True Tone flash off",
      "style": "Photorealistic, influencer aesthetic, high definition, 48MP ProRAW, Photonic Engine processing, sharp focus",
      "vibe": "Casual luxury, clean girl aesthetic, cozy, morning atmosphere, ultra-wide selfie lens quality"
    }
  }
}

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
